create table [User] (
	Name VARCHAR(50),
	Account VARCHAR(50),
	Password VARCHAR(50),
	Email VARCHAR(50),
	Mobile VARCHAR(50),
	CompanyId INT,
	CompanyName VARCHAR(50),
	State INT,
	UserType INT,
	LastLoginTime DATE,
	CreateTime DATE,
	Create_User_Id INT,
	LastUpdate_User_Id INT,
	LastUpdate_Datetime DATE
);
